<rating>4< /rating>< text>
Torero Stadium is a nicely designed, intimate sports venue on the campus of the University of San Diego. It holds just over 6000, making it adequate for college, high school and smaller professional sports. It is the current home of the San Diego Loyal SC of the USL (United Soccer Leagues) Championship. One thing to note, it is all concrete, so invest in a good, thick cushion.< /text>

<Rating>2<//Rating><Review>This place is not the best party supply store for their lack of organization, high prices, and check out practices.

To start off, they got me with the free parking. I should have known that nothing is free. I saw the sign and thought it would be great. As soon as I walked in I saw how disorganized the place was. The line was already taking up an aisle of the store and boxes where open everywhere. The next issue where the prices, when I know for a fact that other stores had similar pinatas for $15 this place had them starting at 20 and 25 for the two I grabbed. With guilt for already parking there I decided to eat the cost. Several candy and items where similarly very high priced, so this is not the place to come get a bargain. Bedies, the employees grabbing pinatas where kind and helpful even through they didn't have a single clue where any character pinata was. There was zero organization and they were constantly being followed by 4 to 5 customers asking where specific pinatas where.

The biggest issue was a result of the cashier. For such a big warehouse with customers packed like rats along the aisles you would think they would have more than one cashier or their fastest person. The opposite, they had a guy who was comically slow if it wasn't for the 40 minute line wait I had to endure. This was like a SNL sketch, he would scan items and when he didn't know he would ask the owner "Kennia" and then repeat the price to the customer who obviously heard her. They really need to get someone that can check the customers out quickly and efficiently so the store can clear out. Last but most importantly they imposed a made up fee on my cc for using a certain card. They said they were being charged that by the credit card, and they were passing the charge onto me. As a merchant that is the cost of doing business, you don't punish me for paying with legal tender in credit card form.

If you are looking for party supplies at a reasonable price, avoid this tourist trap. The free parking comes out more expensive with their unreasonably high prices and credit card fees.< /Review><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< resp>

< text>
Came here for Wine Wednesday and had a blast on the happy hour specials... enjoyed some vino and the boilermakers (Pilsner + Bourbon)... my friend had a classy gin based well and lavish pizza bread.... she was in love with it... as most pizza lovers are...

The Oak and Vine is a very mood lit... has great music and even better service.

They do wine flight specials after 9pm and have a vegan option or two on the menu. A lot of stuff can be made vegan or is vegan friendly, but they don't have a major item aside from olives.

Parking is pretty decent and nearby as there are a couple shared lots that are extremely walkable... street p is rare... but they don't validate.

Overall recommend this place for any type of hang as they have ales, brew and beverages of all kinds.</text>

<user_id>108966298550880155959</user_id><name>Hottesome<//name><Time>1576343900788< /Time>< Rate>

<review>Stopped in recently after a long time away and feel back in love with the Oak and Vine.

A party for six quickly turned into a party for two with all the holiday traffic, but there is parking very close by in a structure unfortunately O & V don't validate.

This wine bar bistro has amazing ambience a great happy hour and lots of pairing eats. Not many vegan options (sigh) but some things that can be made vegan friendly with a heads up.

Drinks are stiff however wonderful. We had amazing service (Ben is the best) and mostly great drinks not a fan of the house red (Cupcake) but do love their wine flight special after 9pm.

Definitely make a reservation if you're in a large party as seating inside and on the patio is limited and they will and want to accommodate you.</review>< pics>

Came here on a Saturday night to enjoy jazz, and we were not disappointed! The musicians were amazing. Simply tremendous! However, it took a while to hear them play because the server who greeted us didn‚Äôt know when the music would start. It would have been nice to know it started at 930pm versus 8-830pm like we were told on the phone.

The flatbread pizzas were good but seemed to be made from canned ingredients and pre-made bread.  No problem. Just don‚Äôt charge $12 for it. I‚Äôd suggest eating before you come.

The wine menu is very good. The options have been selected with care. Obviously, the prices are higher, but you can find some good options here. Beers are $8, which seems excessive considering most of the options. The cocktails are beautiful and prepared with the utmost care. < Review>
We bought all new appliances from valley oak when we moved into our new house. We thought buying from a local place would mean that we would get good service. We were very wrong. We've had nothing but problems with this company. We have had to have service calls for two different appliances because they were installed incorrectly. And each time the service person came out and fixed the issue he was surprised that they were installed so poorly. The final straw was when our new but just out of warranty dishwasher broke. The service person said it would take a $500 repair in a 6-week wait for a part and they just assumed that we would pay that when a brand new dishwasher is not much more expensive. We ended up contacting the manufacturer ourselves and discovered that this was a common faulty issue and that they were covering it free under an extended warranty. Valley oak made no mention of knowing that this was a common problem nor that there was an extended warranty that the manufacturer was covering. We ended up getting it fixed by a different local company that provided exceptional customer service and all of the costs were covered by the manufacturer. I'll never return to valley oak. I think it's awful that we spent so much money with this company and they treated us like this. I cannot recommend them</Review>

<user>115000045179294107182<//user>< review>
I've been living in a studio apartment for about 6 months at Aire now. I'm a single bachelor in my mid-late 20s working in tech and enjoying the outdoors. It's the cheapest studio I found when searching North San Jose and the greater Santa Clara area. The unique design offers a divider between the resting and lounge/relaxation area, which compartmentalizes the unit making it feel less overwhelming.

Thus far, it's been a wholesome positive living experience. I live on the 2nd floor, steps away from the garbage/recycling chute (which is a separate room on its own), from my parking location (via stairs) and the amenities - lounge, pool, gym, which are all of utmost quality. The apartment is fairly isolated from any noise in the hallways. The demographic is mainly young couples or families from what I've observed.

I haven't had any major technical issues. My fire alarm unit became detached suddenly, but all I had to do was e-mail management and they fixed it asap when they did their routine inspection. Paperwork and payments are all done via online (make sure to register your bank account/chequings to avoid unnecessary processing fees for e.g. if you paid via credit card).

Although the staff are busy, they are friendly and competent - I've had wonderful interactions with Shokhou and Taylor, who've been prompt in helping me answer any questions, any requests (for e.g. getting keys to Internet hub room for Internet service provider technicians for Internet set-up), or provide me any necessary paperwork. Most of all, they've been gracious in helping me with my transition from Canada to San Jose via remote communication over the phone, from the self check-in instructions on a weekend night, to any follow-up inquiries I had.

Simply, Aire is a wicked place to live. :)<//review>

We have been renting in different apartments/complexes. This means we have worked with several community management groups. But we have had a very vary pleasant experience with Berkshire Community group, especially The Rey apartments in San Diego and the Aire apartments in San Jose. I will explain why/how. We were renting in the Aire in San Jose and we still had 6 months to the end of my lease that we had to move to San Diego due to job relocation. However, the management in the Aire (Marzieh) was kindly helped us through the process of re-renting from the other Berkshire community group in San Diego (The Rey) to avoid paying any extra fee. Further, they didn't deduct unreasonable amount from our deposit for cleaning (actually it was the least I have ever paid and very clear charges).
At the Rey in San Diego, we had so much fun in the apartment and its amenities. Further, it was always easy to fix a little issues since the management team is VERY responsive, helpful, and responsible. Again for our second lease there was a situation that we had to break our lease and leave to different location. in this situation I was communicating with the management team (Sarah and Justin) to try to rent out our apartment ASAP to avoid paying any fee. It was not the easiest time, but again thanks to Sarah and Justin (and the whole team) we had a very smooth transitioning and our apartment was rented out in less than a week (which means we ended up paying the minimum breaking lease fee).

All in all,  we had a great time living in both Berkshire communities. I believe the main reason is that their staff are very nice and helpful and they have a great culture of customer service.</review>

< Review>
I love taking my kids to Elite vs any other ER or urgent care in the area. It's super convenient and the staff is phenominal. They can do just about anything from lab work, stitches, IVs to basic antibiotics. The only negative thing for me, especially with kids...is the wait time. The lobby can be empty and you should still plan on at least an hour. Patients get called back in a timely manner but I've never spent less than an hour there, sometimes more.  I understand they have a lot of services they provide but everything just seems to take way longer than they average urgent care, even if its a basic ear infection.

The staff outweighs the wait time however for me . I took my middle boy in for a laceration to the foot..in the hectic rush to get my 8 month old and other kid dropped off on the way to urgent care, I left my wallet in the diaper bag. I thought we were stuck with no insurance card and no copay... the receptionist and doctor were awesome and allowed me to give them the information from my babysitter over the phone!</Review>
